   <script>\n397\t        // Session and surface IDs from URL params or generate new\n398\t        const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);\n399\t        const sessionId = }\n414\t\n415\t        function formatStaleness(seconds) {\n416\t            if (seconds < 60) return 'just now';\n417\t            if (seconds < 3600) return `${Math.floor(seconds / 60)}m ago`;\n418\t            if (seconds < 86400) return `${Math.floor(seconds / 3600)}h ago`;\n419\t            return `${Math.floor(seconds / 86400)}d ago`;\n420\t        }\n421\t\n422\t        function getStalenessLevel(seconds) {\n423\t            if (seconds < 600) return 'fresh';      // 10 minutes\n424\t            if (seconds < 3600) return 'stale';     // 1 hour\n425\t            return 'very-stale';\n426\t        }\n427\t\n428\t        function createTopicCard(cardData) {\n429\t            const topic = cardData.topic;\n430\t            const staleness = cardData.staleness;\n431\t            const latestResult = cardData.latest_result;\n432\t\n433\t            const card = document.createElement('div');\n434\t            card.className = 'topic-card';\n435\t const typeClass = topic.type || 'adhoc';\n441\t\n442\t            let html = `\n443\t                <div class=\"topic-header\">\n444\t                    <div `;\n448\t\n449\t            // Add latest result if available\n450\t            if (latestResult) {\n451\t                const urgencyClass = latestResult.urgency || 'normal';\n452\t ${escapeHtml(latestResult.summary)}\n456\t                            <span class=\"urgency-badge ${urgencyClass}\">${urgencyClass}</span>\n457\t                        </div>\n458\t                `;\n459\t\n460\t                if (latestResult.data) {\n461\t                    html += `<div class=\"result-data\">${escapeHtml(JSON.stringify(latestResult.data, null, 2))}</div>`;\n462\t                }\n463\t\n464\t                html += `</div>`;\n465\t            }\n466\t\n467\t            // Add staleness indicator\n468\t            const timeAgo = return div.innerHTML;\n484\t        }\n485\t\n486\t        function updateConnectionStatus(status, text) {\n487\t            const dot = document.getElementById('statusDot');\n488\t            const   function showWorkloadSummary(summary) {\n495\t            const el = document.getElementById('workloadSummary');\n496\t            const parts = [];\n497\t\n498\t            if (summary.pending_intents > 0) {\n499\t                parts.push(`<strong>${summary.pending_intents}</strong> pending intents`);\n500\t            }\n501\t            if (summary.new_results > 0) {\n502\t                parts.push(`<strong>${summary.new_results}</strong> new results`);\n503\t            }\n504\t            if (summary.unresolved_exceptions > 0) {\n505\t                parts.push(`<strong>${summary.unresolved_exceptions}</strong> unresolved exceptions`);\n506\t            }\n507\t\n508\t            if (parts.length > 0) {\n509\t                el.innerHTML = '📊   }\n515\t\n516\t        async function registerSurface() {\n517\t            try {\n518\t                const response = await fetch('/api/v1/surfaces/register', {\n519\t                    method: {\n533\t                console.error('Error registering surface:', error);\n534\t                throw error;\n535\t            }\n536\t        }\n537\t\n538\t        async function loadTopics() {\n539\t            try {\n540\t                const response = await fetch(`/api/v1/sessions/${sessionId}/topics`);\n541\t                if (!response.ok) return;\n542\t\n543\t                const     const result = JSON.parse(event.data);\n593\t                console.log('New result:', result);\n594\t                loadTopics(); // Reload topics to show new result\n595\t }).catch(console.error);\n622\t            }\n623\t        }, 30000); // Every 30 seconds\n624\t\n625\t        // ── Input bar ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n626\t\n627\t        const textarea = document.getElementById('inputTextarea');\n628\t        const btnSend  = document.getElementById('btnSend');\n629\t        const btnMic   = textarea.value = '';\n653\t            textarea.style.height = 'auto';\n654\t            btnSend.disabled = true;\n655\t\n656\t            try {\n657\t                const resp = await Speech API mic\n672\t        let recognition = null;\n673\t\n674\t        if ('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window || 'SpeechRecognition' in window) {\n675\t            const SpeechRecognition = recognition.interimResults = true;\n679\t            recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n680\t\n681\t            let finalTranscript = '';\n682\t\n683\t            recognition.onstart = () => {\n684\t                btnMic.classList.add('recording');\n685\t                finalTranscript = textarea.value;\n686\t            };\n687\t\n688\t            recognition.onresult = (e) => {\n689\t e.results[i][0].transcript;\n693\t                    } else {\n694\t                        interim += e.results[i][0].transcript;\n695\t                    }\n696\t                }\n697\t       }\n\n        function formatStaleness(seconds) {\n            if (seconds < 60) return 'just now';\n            if (seconds < 3600) return `${Math.floor(seconds / 60)}m ago`;\n            if (seconds < 86400) return `${Math.floor(seconds / 3600)}h ago`;\n            return `${Math.floor(seconds / 86400)}d ago`;\n        }\n\n        function getStalenessLevel(seconds) {\n            if (seconds < 600) return 'fresh';      // 10 minutes\n            if (seconds < 3600) return 'stale';     // 1 hour\n            return 'very-stale';\n        }\n\n        function card = document.createElement('div');\n            card.className = 'topic-card';\n            card.dataset.topicId = topic.id;\n\n            const stalenessLevel = getStalenessLevel(staleness.seconds);\n            card.classList.add(stalenessLevel);\n\n            const typeClass = topic.type || 'adhoc';\n\n            let html = `\n                <div }\n\n        function updateConnectionStatus(status, text) {\n            const dot = document.getElementById('statusDot');\n            const statusText = document.getElementById('statusText');\n\n            dot.className = 'status-dot ' + status;\n            statusText.textContent = text;\n        }\n\n        function showWorkloadSummary(summary) {\n            const el = (summary.unresolved_exceptions > 0) {\n                parts.push(`<strong>${summary.unresolved_exceptions}</strong> unresolved exceptions`);\n            }\n\n            if (parts.length > 0) {\n                el.innerHTML = '📊 While you were away: ' + parts.join(', ');\n                el.classList.add('show');\n            } else {\n                el.classList.remove('show');\n            }\n         <p>Topics will appear here as you interact with ADC.</p>\n                        </div>\n                    `;\n                    return;\n                }\n\n       async function dispatch(utterance) {\n            if (!utterance) return;\n            textarea.value = '';\n            textarea.style.height = 'auto';\n            btnSend.disabled = true;\n\n            try {\n                const resp = await fetch('/dispatch', {\n                    method: 'POST',\n                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n console.error('Dispatch error:', err);\n                }\n            } catch (err) {\n                console.error('Dispatch failed:', err);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Web Speech API mic\n        let recognition = null;\n\n        if ('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window || 'SpeechRecognition' in window) {\n            const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n\n            let finalTranscript = '';\n\n            recognition.onstart = () => {\n                btnMic.classList.add('recording');\n                finalTranscript =         if (e.results[i].isFinal) {\n                        finalTranscript += e.results[i][0].transcript;\n                    } else {\n                        interim +=       }\n\n        function formatStaleness(seconds) {\n            if (seconds < 60) return 'just now';\n            if (seconds < 3600) return `${Math.floor(seconds / 60)}m ago`;\n            if (seconds < 86400) return `${Math.floor(seconds / 3600)}h ago`;\n            return `${Math.floor(seconds / 86400)}d ago`;\n        }\n\n        function getStalenessLevel(seconds) {\n            if (seconds < 600) return 'fresh';      // 10 minutes\n            if (seconds < 3600) return 'stale';     // 1 hour\n            return 'very-stale';\n        }\n\n        function card = document.createElement('div');\n            card.className = 'topic-card';\n            card.dataset.topicId = topic.id;\n\n            const stalenessLevel = getStalenessLevel(staleness.seconds);\n            card.classList.add(stalenessLevel);\n\n            const typeClass = topic.type || 'adhoc';\n\n            let html = `\n                <div class=\"topic-header\">\n                    <div class=\"topic-label\">${escapeHtml(topic.label)}</div>\n                    <span class=\"topic-type ${typeClass}\">${topic.type || 'adhoc'}</span>\n                </div>\n            `;\n\n            // Add latest result if available\n            if (latestResult) {\n                const urgencyClass = latestResult.urgency || 'normal';\n                html += `\n                    <div class=\"result-content\">\n                        <div class=\"result-summary\">\n                            ${escapeHtml(latestResult.summary)}\n                            <span class=\"urgency-badge ${urgencyClass}\">${urgencyClass}</span>\n                        </div>\n                `;\n\n                if (latestResult.data) {\n                    html += `<div class=\"result-data\">${escapeHtml(JSON.stringify(latestResult.data, null, 2))}</div>`;\n                }\n\n                html += `</div>`;\n            }\n\n            // Add <span class=\"staleness-dot ${stalenessLevel}\"></span>\n                    <span>Updated ${timeAgo}</span>\n                </div>\n            `;\n\n            card.innerHTML = html;\n }\n\n        function updateConnectionStatus(status, text) {\n            const dot = document.getElementById('statusDot');\n            const statusText = document.getElementById('statusText');\n\n            dot.className = 'status-dot ' + status;\n            statusText.textContent = text;\n        }\n\n        function showWorkloadSummary(summary) {\n            const el = document.getElementById('workloadSummary');\n            const parts = [];\n\n            if (summary.pending_intents > 0) {\n                parts.push(`<strong>${summary.pending_intents}</strong> pending intents`);\n            }\n            if (summary.new_results > 0) {\n                parts.push(`<strong>${summary.new_results}</strong> new results`);\n            }\n            if (summary.unresolved_exceptions > 0) {\n                parts.push(`<strong>${summary.unresolved_exceptions}</strong> unresolved exceptions`);\n            }\n\n            if (parts.length > 0) {\n                el.innerHTML = '📊 While you were away: ' + parts.join(', ');\n                el.classList.add('show');\n            } else {\n                el.classList.remove('show');\n            }\n        }\n\n        async function registerSurface() {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch('/api/v1/surfaces/register', {\n                    method: 'POST',\n                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n                    body: JSON.stringify({\n                        session_id: sessionId,\n                        surface_type: (!response.ok) return;\n\n                const data = await response.json();\n                const container = document.getElementById('topicsContainer');\n\n                if (!data.cards || data.cards.length === 0) {\n                    container.innerHTML = `\n                        <div class=\"empty-state\">\n                            <h2>No active topics</h2>\n                            <p>Topics will appear here as you interact with ADC.</p>\n                        </div>\n                    `;\n                    return;\n                }\n\n                container.innerHTML = '';\n                data.cards.forEach(cardData => {\n                    container.appendChild(createTopicCard(cardData));\n                });\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error('Error loading topics:', error);\n            }\n        }\n\n        function connectSSE() {\n            updateConnectionStatus('connecting', 'Connecting...');\n\n            const url = `/api/v1/sse?surface_id=${encodeURIComponent(surfaceId)}&session_id=${encodeURIComponent(sessionId)}&surface_type=${encodeURIComponent(surfaceType)}`;\n            eventSource = new EventSource(url);\n\n            eventSource.onopen = () => {\n                updateConnectionStatus('', 'Connected');\n                loadTopics();\n            };\n\n            eventSource.onerror = (error) => {\n                console.error('SSE error:', error);\n                updateConnectionStatus('disconnected', 'Disconnected');\n            };\n\n            eventSource.addEventListener('connected', (event) => {\n                const data = JSON.parse(event.data);\n                console.log('SSE connected:', data);\n            });\n\n            eventSource.addEventListener('workload_summary', (event) => {\n                const summary = JSON.parse(event.data);\n                showWorkloadSummary(summary);\n            });\n\n            eventSource.addEventListener('result_created', (event) => {\n                const result = JSON.parse(event.data);\n                console.log('New result:', result);\n                loadTopics(); console.log('Topic updated:', topic);\n                loadTopics();\n            });\n\n            eventSource.addEventListener('disconnect', (event) => {\n                const data =       async function dispatch(utterance) {\n            if (!utterance) return;\n            textarea.value = '';\n            textarea.style.height = 'auto';\n            btnSend.disabled = true;\n\n            try {\n                const resp = await fetch('/dispatch', {\n                    method: 'POST',\n                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n                    body: JSON.stringify({ utterance, session_id: sessionId }),\n                });\n                if (!resp.ok) {\n                    const err = await resp.text();\n                    console.error('Dispatch error:', err);\n                }\n            } catch (err) {\n                console.error('Dispatch failed:', err);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Web Speech API mic\n        let recognition = null;\n\n        if ('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window || 'SpeechRecognition' in window) {\n            const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;\n            recognition = new SpeechRecognition();\n            recognition.continuous = false;\n            recognition.interimResults = true;\n            recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n\n            let finalTranscript = '';\n\n            recognition.onstart = () => {\n                btnMic.classList.add('recording');\n                finalTranscript = textarea.value;\n            };\n\n            recognition.onresult = (e) => {\n                let interim = '';\n                for (let i = e.resultIndex; i < e.results.length; i++) {\n
